PRADESHIYA SABHA  - POLPITHIGAMA
IT is hereby notiﬁ ed for the public information that it has been decided under Resolution No. 632 of the Resolution Book 
No. 01  and dated 17.07.2023 that the roads and thoroughfares included in the schedule below should be declared as roads 
and thoroughfares   owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Polpithigama, in addition to the Gazette Notiﬁ cation No. 2289/38 and 
dated 21.07.2022,  in terms of the purposes assigned to the Pradeshiya Sabhas of the North-West Province by the series 
of “Orders on the preparation of plans and publishing  notices specifying the list of names of the roads and thoroughfares  
maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabhas of the North-West Province”, published in the Extraordinary Gazette Noti ﬁ cation 
No. 2238/35 dated 30th   July 2021 by the Hon. Governor in the North Western Province  to be read with Section 24 of the 
Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987.
It is hereby further notiﬁ ed that, if it is the opinion of the party claiming the said land that any road or thoroughfare included 
in the said schedule passes through any land or a part of any land of that party, a case should be ﬁ led in the competent Court 
to prove his right to the said land before the expiry of a period of three months from the date of this notiﬁ cation.
It is further notiﬁ ed that every road and thoroughfare included in the said schedule, against which a legal action has not 
been taken before the expiry of the said period of three months shall be deemed to be a road or a thoroughfare which has 
been vested in the Polpithigama  Pradeshiya Sabha.
W.G.N
ISHANTHA KUMARA,
Secretary , 
Pradeshiya Sabha Polpithigama.
18th  July 2026
At the Head Ofﬁ ce of Pradeshiya Sabha Polpithigama.

Decision 
Pradeshiya Sabha Polpithigama hereby decides, that the roads and thoroughfares mentioned in the schedule below should be considered as roads and thoroughfares 
maintained by the Pradeshiya sabha Polpithigama, in terms of the provisions in the  Extraordinary Gazette Paper No. 2317/87 and dated 03rd February in 2023 
published by the Hon. Governor in the North Western Province, and the  orders made under the series of  “Orders on the preparation of plans and publishing  notices 
specifying the list of names of the roads and thoroughfares  maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabhas of the North-West Province”, p ublished in the Extraordinary 
Gazette Notiﬁ cation No. 2238/35 dated 30th July 2021 by the Hon. Governor in the North Western Province by virtue of powers vested  under  Section 24 (1)  of 
the Pradeshiya Sabha Act No. 15 of 1987.
